      <article class="post-8698 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-recipe tag-chicken tag-kraft-canada tag-main-dish tag-recipe entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         Family Favourite Recipe: Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas #whatscooking
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2014-11-06T14:05:24+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          November 6, 2014
         </time>
         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://littlemisskate.ca/author/kate/" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Kate
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://littlemisskate.ca/recipe/family-favourite-recipe-fiesta-chicken-enchiladas-whatscooking/#comments">
           21 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <a href="http://littlemisskate.ca/recipe/family-favourite-recipe-fiesta-chicken-enchiladas-whatscooking/" title="Family Favourite Recipe: Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas #whatscooking">
        <img alt="easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-2" class="post-image" height="693" src="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-2-1024x693.jpg" width="1024"/>
       </a>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <input data-frizzlyhovercontainer="" data-frizzlypostcontainer="" data-frizzlyposttitle="Family Favourite Recipe: Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas #whatscooking" data-frizzlyposturl="http://littlemisskate.ca/recipe/family-favourite-recipe-fiesta-chicken-enchiladas-whatscooking/" type="hidden" value=""/>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          Have you ever made a meal where it has been eaten so quickly that the kids are done before you even sit down for your first bite? That is exactly what happened when I made Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas this week. Both Little Bear &amp; Monkeys plates were clean and they were asking for more before I even had a single bite of mine! Now I cant really blame them, because the enchiladas were delicious. This recipe uses basic ingredients we always have in our fridge, and was simple to make. But dont let the simplicity fool you, it is a tasty dish that everyone loved. Loved so much in fact there were no leftovers, I guess I should have made double! I adapted the
          <strong>
           <a href="http://www.kraftcanada.com/recipes/fiesta-chicken-enchiladas-made-over-121733" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
            Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas
           </a>
          </strong>
          recipe from Kraft Canada Whats Cooking website and here is what I created:
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          <a href="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-2.jpg">
           <img alt="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" class="aligncenter wp-image-8701" height="338" src="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-2-1024x693.jpg" title="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" width="500"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <br/>
        </p>
        <div class="easyrecipe" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">
         <link href="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-2-1024x693.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
         <div class="ERSRatings" itemprop="aggregateRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating">
          <div class="ERSRatingOuter">
           <div class="ERSRatingInner" style="width: 100%">
           </div>
           <div class="review">
            <span class="rating">
             <span class="average" itemprop="ratingValue">
              5.0
             </span>
             from
             <span class="count" itemprop="ratingCount">
              5
             </span>
             reviews
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="ERSSavePrint">
          <span class="ERSPrintBtnSpan">
           <a class="ERSPrintBtn" href="http://littlemisskate.ca/easyrecipe-print/8698-0/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
            Print
           </a>
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="ERSName" itemprop="name">
          Fiesta Chicken Enchiladas
         </div>
         <div class="ERSClear">
         </div>
         <div class="ERSDetails">
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
          <div class="ERSTimes">
          </div>
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="ERSIngredients">
          <div class="ERSIngredientsHeader ERSHeading">
           Ingredients
          </div>
          <ul>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            2 Tbsp Cooking Oil
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            2 Chicken breasts - cooked and shredded
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            2 Peppers - Sliced thinly, I used red and orange
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            1 Onion - sliced thinly
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            1 Clove of garlic - minced
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            1 Tbsp. chili powder
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            2 cups of Cooked rice - about 1 cup of uncooked rice
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             cup salsa, divided
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             of 250-g pkg.Philadelphia Light Brick Cream Cheese Spread, cubed
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             cup Kraft Tex Mex Light Shredded Cheese, divided
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
            6 large whole wheat tortillas
           </li>
          </ul>
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="ERSInstructions">
          <div class="ERSInstructionsHeader ERSHeading">
           Instructions
          </div>
          <ol>
           <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
            Heat oven to 375F.
           </li>
           <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
            Heat oil in a large skillet on medium heat. Add cooked chicken, peppers, onions, garlic and chili powder; cook and stir 8 min.
           </li>
           <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
            Stir in  cup salsa (you may need more if you are using chunky salsa), rice, and cream cheese spread; cook and stir 3 to 5 min. or until cream cheese is melted and mixture is well blended. Stir in  cup shredded cheese.
           </li>
           <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
            Spoon heaping  cup chicken mixture down centre of each tortilla; roll up. Place, seam sides down, in 13x9-inch baking dish sprayed with cooking spray; top with remaining salsa and shredded cheese.
           </li>
           <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
            Bake 20 min. or until heated through - Enjoy!
           </li>
          </ol>
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="endeasyrecipe" style="display: none" title="style001">
          3.2.2802
         </div>
        </div>
        <br/>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          Even just thinking about them now is making me hungry! With the salsa and cream cheese the chicken mixture stays nice and moist during baking. If you like a little more spice to your meals you can use a medium or hot salsa.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          <a href="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-1.jpg">
           <img alt="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" class="aligncenter wp-image-8702" height="363" src="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-1-1024x743.jpg" title="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" width="500"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          I think the nice time I makeFiesta Chicken Enchiladas I would also add in 1 cup of drained canned corn to include even more veggies in them. But even as they are now, they have become a family favourite and are a perfect way to use up leftover cooked chicken as well.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          <a href="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-3.jpg">
           <img alt="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" class="aligncenter wp-image-8703" height="454" src="http://littlemisskate.ca/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/easy-Chicken-Enchiladas-recipe-3-1024x928.jpg" title="easy Chicken Enchiladas recipe" width="500"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
          Need some more dinner time inspiration? There are tons more mouth-watering
          <a href="http://www.kraftcanada.com/en/recipes/dinner/chicken-recipes/casseroles.aspx" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
           chicken casserole recipes
          </a>
          including Chicken &amp; Roasted Red Potatoes or Bruschetta Chicken Bake on the Krafts Whats Cooking website. You can also be tempted with delicious looking pictures by following Whats Cooking on
          <a href="http://instagram.com/kraftwhatscooking" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
           Instagram
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/whatscookingkft/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
           Pinterest
          </a>
          .
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: 10pt;">
          <em>
           Disclosure: I am part of the Krafts Whats Cooking ambassador program. All opinions are strictly my own.
          </em>
         </span>
        </p>

/*  Collapse Functions, version 2.0
 *
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
String.prototype.trim = function() {
  return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
}

function createCookie(name,value,days) {
  if (days) {
    var date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
  } else {
    var expires = "";
  }
  document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
      c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function eraseCookie(name) {
  createCookie(name,"",-1);
}

function addExpandCollapse(id, expandSym, collapseSym, accordion) {
  jQuery('#' + id + ' span.expand').live('click', function() {
    if (accordion==1) {
      var theDiv = jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').parent().children('div');
      jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
      jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
      createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
      jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.sym').html(expandSym);
      //jQuery('#' + id + ' .expand .sym').html(expandSym);
    }
    expandArch(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
  jQuery('#' + id + ' span.collapse').live('click', function() {
    collapseArch(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
}

function expandArch(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().children('div');
    try {
      if (collapsItems[jQuery(theDiv).attr('id')]!='') {
        jQuery(theDiv).html(collapsItems[jQuery(theDiv).attr('id')]).show('normal');
      } else {
        jQuery(theDiv).show('normal');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      jQuery(theDiv).show('normal');
    }
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('expand').addClass('collapse');
    jQuery(symbol).children('.sym').html(collapseSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 1, 7);
}
function collapseArch(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().children('div');
    jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
    jQuery(symbol).children('.sym').html(expandSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
}
addExpandCollapse('widget-collapsarch-4-top','&#x25BA;', '&#x25BC;', 0)// ]]&gt;
              </script>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
